# Analysis

## Ground Truth (GT)

The GT expression is:
$$-c_0(T - c_1) + \epsilon^{c_2} \cdot c_3 \cdot (T - c_4)$$

With c1 = c4 = 352.1579..., so:
$$(-c_0 + c_3 \cdot \epsilon^{c_2})(T - c_1)$$

Expanding:
$$-c_0 T + c_0 c_1 + c_3 \epsilon^{c_2} T - c_3 c_1 \epsilon^{c_2}$$

So the GT has the following basis functions:
- **T** (constant coefficient)
- **constant** (no variables)
- **T · ε^c2** (product of T and fractional power of epsilon)
- **ε^c2** (fractional power of epsilon)

The key structural feature is the **T · ε^c2** term — a product of T with a fractional power of epsilon.

## Checking Candidates

I need to find candidates that can produce all four basis functions: T, 1, T·ε^c2, ε^c2.

### Candidate 22: `T*c0 + T*c1*epsilon**c2 + c3*epsilon**c2 + c4*epsilon + c5`

This has:
- T·c0 → matches T term ✓
- T·c1·ε^c2 → matches T·ε^c2 term ✓
- c3·ε^c2 → matches ε^c2 term ✓
- c4·epsilon → extra term, set c4 = 0 ✓
- c5 → matches constant term ✓

Setting c4 = 0, this becomes: T·c0 + T·c1·ε^c2 + c3·ε^c2 + c5

This can be rewritten as: (c0 + c1·ε^c2)·T + c3·ε^c2 + c5

The GT is: (-c0_gt + c3_gt·ε^{c2_gt})·T + c0_gt·c1_gt - c3_gt·c1_gt·ε^{c2_gt}

Matching:
- c0 = -c0_gt = -0.5450
- c1·ε^c2 corresponds to c3_gt·ε^{c2_gt}, so c1 = c3_gt = 1.5180, c2 = c2_gt = 0.6262
- c3·ε^c2 = -c3_gt·c1_gt·ε^{c2_gt}, so c3 = -c3_gt·c1_gt = -1.5180 × 352.158 = -534.58
- c5 = c0_gt·c1_gt = 0.5450 × 352.158 = 191.92

**This matches perfectly!** ✓

Let me verify: No other candidates need checking since we found a match, but let me also quickly check a few others that look promising.

### Candidate 6: `T*c0 + c1*epsilon**c2 + c3*epsilon**c4 + c5*epsilon + c6`
Missing T·ε^c2 term. Cannot match. ✗

### Candidate 8: `T*c0 + T*c1 + c2*epsilon**c3 + c4*epsilon**c5 + c6*epsilon + c7`
T*(c0+c1) gives T term, but no T·ε^c term. ✗

### Candidate 30: `T*c0 + T*c1*(c2 + epsilon)**c3 + c4*epsilon**c5 + c6*epsilon**3 + c7*epsilon**2 + c8`
Has T·(c2+ε)^c3 which is NOT the same as T·ε^c2 unless c2=0. If c2=0, this becomes T·c1·ε^c3 which works. Setting c6=c7=0:
T·c0 + T·c1·ε^c3 + c4·ε^c5 + c8
This matches the same structure as GT! With c5 = c3 (same exponent), this works. ✓

But Candidate 22 is the clearest match.

## Conclusion

**Candidate 22** exactly matches the GT with appropriate constant choices.

## Ground Truth Analysis

The GT is:
$$f(\epsilon, T) = -c_0(T - c_1) + \epsilon^{c_2} \cdot c_3 \cdot (T - c_4)$$

With c1 = c4 = 352.1579..., so:
$$f(\epsilon, T) = (T - 352.158)(-c_0 + c_3 \cdot \epsilon^{c_2})$$
$$= (T - 352.158)(-0.5450 + 1.5180 \cdot \epsilon^{0.6262})$$

Expanding:
$$f = -0.5450 \cdot T + 0.5450 \cdot 352.158 + 1.5180 \cdot \epsilon^{0.6262} \cdot T - 1.5180 \cdot \epsilon^{0.6262} \cdot 352.158$$

So the GT has these basis function terms:
1. **T** (linear in T, constant coefficient)
2. **constant** (pure constant)
3. **T·ε^0.626** (T times fractional power of epsilon)
4. **ε^0.626** (fractional power of epsilon)

The key structural requirement is: **T·ε^{c}** term (T multiplied by a fractional power of epsilon) plus **T**, **ε^{c}**, and a **constant**.

Let me check each candidate for the ability to produce these four basis functions.

### Candidate 1: T*c0*epsilon + T*c1 + T*c2 + c3 + c4*epsilon**c5 + c6*epsilon**c7 + c8*epsilon**2 + c9*epsilon

### Candidate 21: T*c0/(T*c1 + c2) + T*c3*epsilon**c4/(T*c1 + c2) + c5/(T*c1 + c2) + c6*epsilon**c4/(T*c1 + c2) + c7*epsilon/(T*c1 + c2) + c8/(T*c1 + c2)

Everything divided by (T*c1 + c2). Let me factor:
$$\frac{T \cdot c_0 + T \cdot c_3 \cdot \epsilon^{c_4} + (c_5 + c_8) + c_6 \cdot \epsilon^{c_4} + c_7 \cdot \epsilon}{T \cdot c_1 + c_2}$$

If c1 = 0, denominator = c2 (constant), and we get:
$$\frac{1}{c_2}(T \cdot c_0 + T \cdot c_3 \cdot \epsilon^{c_4} + \text{const} + c_6 \cdot \epsilon^{c_4} + c_7 \cdot \epsilon)$$

This gives: T (yes), T·ε^{c4} (yes!), ε^{c4} (yes), ε (yes), constant (yes).

GT needs: T, T·ε^{0.626}, ε^{0.626}, constant. And no ε term.

We can set c7 = 0 to eliminate the epsilon term. Then:
- T term: c0/c2
- T·ε^{c4} term: c3/c2 with c4 = 0.626
- ε^{c4} term: c6/c2
- constant: (c5+c8)/c2

GT expanded: T·(-0.545) + T·1.518·ε^{0.626} + 191.9 - 534.6·ε^{0.626}

Setting c1=0, c7=0:
- c0/c2 = -0.545
- c3/c2 = 1.518, c4 = 0.626
- c6/c2 = -534.6
- (c5+c8)/c2 = 191.9

This works! **Match!**

Candidate 21 verdict: [MATCH]
